sdug bsngal rgyun mi 'chad pa bsten 'tshal lo / /
zhes sogs dang /
'dul ba lung las /
bsags pa kun gyi mtha' 'dzad cing / /
mthon po rnams kyi mtha' ltung 'gyur / /
phrad pa'i mtha' ni 'bral ba ste / /
gson pa'i mtha' ni 'chi ba yin / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar 'khor ba'i phun tshogs ji 'dra zhig thob kyang mtha' rgyud pas ma bsdus pa med pas mi yul gyi bde skyid lta zhog /
tshangs pa /
brgya byin /
'khor los sgyur rgyal gyi dpal 'byor thob kyang mi brtan pa'i rang bzhin /
ltung ba'i chos can /
bslu ba'i chos can /
thar pa'i bar gcod /
ngan song gi sdug bsngal mi bzad pa 'dren par byed pa las /
gtan gyi 'dun mar phan pa'i snying po cung zad tsam yang med nges kyi ngang tshul thugs kyi mthil du bzungs te thugs pham cung zad kyang mi bzhes pa nas /
sku che dang sku lus la bsngo ba ma byung ba 'dis slad da dung gtan 'dun snying po'i spros ba ji 'dra zhig bzhed kyang bsgrub tu yod pa ni /
sa @# / /
skya legs bshad las /
chen po re zhig rgud gyur kyang / /
de la gdung ba bskyed mi dgos / /
zla ba re zhig gzas zin kyang / /
de ma thag tu grol bar 'gyur / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar thugs bde'i dpyid du rol ba /
nyams bzhes zhal 'don shog lhe zur stsal ltar shin tu 'thus nges dang /
de thog bla ma mchod pa re nyams bzhes grub na mdo sngags yongs rdzogs kyi gnad bsdus cha tshang ba dang /
dga' ldan snyan brgyud sprul pa'i glegs bam gyi man ngag gi mthil phyung ba lta bu yin cing /
grub chen chos rdo rje dang /
rgyal ba dben sa ba sogs kyang 'di nyid thugs dam gyi mthil du mdzad nas tshe gcig la zung 'jug gi go 'phang brnyes pa sogs rang lugs dam pa gong ma thams cad kyi thugs dam gyi mthil /
tshig nyung /
'dus che /
byin che /
zab gnad che ba bcas re zhig de tsam dang /
slar de thog 'jigs byed dpa' gcig dang /
rdo rje rnal 'byor ma re nyams bzhes bskyang grub na zab myur khyad par du mas lhag pa bcas brtse rol /
gang ltar chos lugs grub mtha' chal chol rtag chad kyi g.yang sar gzhol ba rnams la dbu 'khor na sku tshe gtan gyi 'dun ma rtsa nor gyi steng du /
sku tshe 'dir yang mdzad 'phrin lam du mi lhong ba yong nges mthong chos ltar lags na rang lugs 'dzam gling bstan pa'i snying po /
tshang lam nor ba /
lta sgom spyod gsum gang gi cha nas kyang grub mtha' gzhan phyogs pa rnams kyis cha tsam yang 'gran pa'i zla thams cad dang bral ba dge ldan ring lugs gceng ma'i rnam thar bsre lhad med par rjes su bskyang na 'phral yun kun gyi bzhed don 'bad med du 'grub pa la gnad che ba kho pos zol med kyis gsol ba thugs kyi mthil du bcang zhing /
thugs dam nyams bzhes kyang gsung rab sgo brgya 'byed? ba'i lde mig gcig chog rgyal po byang chub lam rim rang la chig dril mdzad na de las gnad che med pa bcas zhib par theg chen rin po cher mngags zhus ltar dbyings klong zab mor rol pa / /
! / /
nags shod shug dgon nas stag pu rdo rje 'chang chen por 'bul gnang mdzad pa /
mdo smad bka' chos rgya che'i skabs grub mtha' sna tshogs 'dzoms sar rang gzhan grub mtha'i dgag bzhag phog thug che rigs mi byed pa gal che tshul phebs pa ni thugs brtse sha tsha gting nas ma lhod pa'i bka' slob lhug pa zol med du pha yis bur bzhin rjes gdams snying gi thig ler rang don rang gces kyis rgyun bcang nyag gcig zhus chog pa /
'on kyang spyod 'jug las /
de la 'jig rten phal ba ni / /
rnal 'byor 'jig rten gyis gnod cing / /
rnal 'byor pa yang blo khyod kyis / /
gong ma gong ma rnams kyis gnod / /
ces gsungs pa ltar rang gzhung bsrangs te drang por bkral skabs shugs kyis gzhan la dgag par 'gro rigs ji snyed cig mi 'ong thabs med 'jug pa las /
bstan bcos las dpyad rtsod la chags pa'i phyir / /
ma mdzad rnam grol phyir ni de nyid bstan / /
gal te de nyid rnam par bshad pa na / /
gzhan gzhung 'jig par 'gyur na nyes pa med / /
ces sogs gsungs pa'i rigs dang /
rje'i lam rim che chung rang du'ang bod @# / /
snga rabs pa sogs kyi lta sgom la phyogs snga'i dgag bzhag ji snyed cig mdzad pa rnams rang gzhung 'brel ba'i tshen de de bzhin dum bkral thabs med rigs la bla ma'i bka' bcag pa'i nyes par mi 'gyur ba'i dgongs phrol brtse gzigs /
gzhi rtsa gus rang yang gzhan gyi sgro skur phog thug sogs 'di snang gi grags skam la gnod dogs til 'bru tsam snying thag pa nas ma mchis kyang /
kha zhor gtam zhor du chos spong gi las ngan du 'gyur dogs kyis sems khur stabs gzab smra mkhas rgyun du byed bzhin pa'i khar brtse chen bka' slob snying gi nor bur bcang chog pa bcas brtse chen dgyes klong du rol zhing / /
! / /
bde chen lhun grub steng dgon par gnang ba /
dgon 'di snga dus bka' brgyud dang dge ldan zung du 'brel ba'i lta grub gtsang ma bstan pa'i mig rgyan du che ba zhig yin nges kyang /
bar lam zhig nas phra zhing mdzangs pa'i rnam dpyod kyi mig ldong zhing /
bsod nams kyi mthu dman pa sna tshogs kyis /
yang dag |ltar snang /
dman dang lam gol gyi khyad par ji bzhin ma dpogs pas grub pa'i mtha' 'dra min gyi bsre lhad sna tshogs kyi rkyen la brten bla ma gong ma rnams kyis gang la gnyer du gtad pa'i srung ma'i dbang po rnams 'khu zhing ldogs pas| tshe thung /
nad mang /
bya ba lam du 'gro min sogs mi 'dod rgud pa'i rnam 'gyur ji snyed cig byung dang 'byung 'gyur gyi rtsa ba de rang la thug 'dra bas /
phyin chad blo bzang rgyal ba'i bzhed srol gtsang ma bsre lhad med pa'i rnam thar rjes su bskyangs na legs lam 'byung khyad che nges /
kho bos rang zon do dga'i zol sbyor cung zad tsam gyis kyang ma bslad par lhag bsam zla ba'i spun zla dkar pos snying thag pa nas ched du gsol ba lags kyang /
tshad mas thugs su 'thad pa dang /
phyag len du khel ba ji bzhin dka' snyam yang /
rang khongs ser smad gung ru'i thob khungs la brten sha zhen bzod med kyi gsong bo'i dag la thugs yid rton te ji ltar gsol bzhin phyag len du thebs tshe chos srid sgo kun nas yar rgyas 'byung nges snyam zhing /
gnad dmigs rim gro de lhag ma mchis pa tshang mas rjes su dgongs 'tshal /
'on kyang rkyen sel rim gro nges par bzhed na bla mchod dang 'brel pa'i tshogs khri tshar /
dam tshig rdo rje'i bzlas pa bye ba /
sngon gyi srung ma'i dbang po rnams kyi bskang bshags spyi dang /
lhag par chos rgyal gyi bskang bshags dang 'brel ba'i drug cum stong tshar sogs 'gro che /
nor lug sogs kyi srog gcod spong ba bcas sgrub gnang mdzod /
ngos nas kyang mchog gsum thugs rje bskul ba'i gsol 'debs zhu / /
! / /
rgyal thang rong thang steng sde pa rta mgrin tshe ring la gnang ba /
nyid lhas nas rang yul du phebs rjes dgra 'thab kyi sdig las ma dgos pa zhig e 'ong snyam shin tu re che yang /
der dmag spyi ma bzhugs pas dgra 'thab lan 'gar mdzad dgos byung ba a kha kha snyam rung /
yul gyi bde skyid la phan re'i lhag bsam gyis yin tshe cung e drag snyam /
gang ltar sngon mdzad la 'gyod bshags nan tan dang /
phyin chad de ltar mi dgos par rnam dkar dge ba'i bya bas @# / /
dus 'da' ba zhig 'ong thabs thugs bsam gyi phugs su nan tan bzung bar mdzod cig ces ngos nas bzod med sha tshas snying gtam yin /
mi 'khrugs pa'i sku bzhengs rgyu sdig bshags la mchog tu bsngags pas nges par bzhengs gnang mdzod / /
! drag g.yab grong re'i lde'u 'chang la stsal pa /
deng skabs rang 'og dmag mis dkar min bya ba sna tshogs byung shor thugs pham che ba shin tu mad rung /
sems can rang rang las bskos thog tu babs par thugs ngal mi gnang ba nas /
cung zad zhar drung byung rigs la bshags sdom mdzad pas 'thus shing /
bla brang zhabs zhu sogs spyi bye'i mdzad sgo gang la'ang bstan dang gzhan phan lhag bsam snying bcang gis kun nas bslangs te mdzad na rnam dkar legs tshogs su 'gyur ba yang ches mang bas /
gseng bar gang rnyed zhar dang zhor la nyams bzhes spyi dang /
lhag par byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i dmigs rnam che 'grus chung 'grus su skyong zhing| de yang ngos nas spom mda'i las tshan par phul ba'i skyong tshul gyi man ngag zur chung zhig kyang phul yod / /
! / /
rgyal thang mkhan zur blo bzang rgyal mtshan la gnang ba /
phyi ma'i skye gnas bzang ngan ni /
gtso bor rang rang dkar nag las kyi 'bras bu ji ltar bsags pa'i rjes su dpog pa las /
mo rtsis dang brtag pa sogs la yid brtan bya ba mi rung /
gtso bor tshul khrims kyi bslab pa mthar son cing rnam dag dge sbyor sogs gang nus su mdzad pa 'di dag la bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs nan tan sogs da dung sku tshe'i lhag mar gtan gyi 'dun ma sgrub pa la nan tan 'bad na sku'i skye gnas bzang po zhig tu yong nges / /
! / /
rtse shar bre kha ba nas rnying lugs kyi kha 'don nyams len rnams bskyur gcig bya rtsis la chos spong gi nyes pa 'byung mi 'byung zhes par /
rnying lugs yi dam bzhag ste dge lugs yi dam du bsgyur kyang chos spong gi las su ci la 'gro ste /
sngon mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor kyang dang po bon /
de nas bon bzhag ste rnying ma /
de nas rnying ma bzhag ste sngags gsar ma mdzad pa rnam thar na gsal /
sa chen kun snying yang dang po rnying ma /
de nas rnying ma bzhag ste sngags gsar ma mdzad /
gzhan yang de 'dra ba sa skya /
bka' gdams /
dge lugs sogs kyi phyogs su shin tu mang ba yod pa 'dir 'drir mi lang ba so so'i rnam thar du gsal /
chos lugs so so la yid kyis ma dad log rtog byas na chos spong du 'gro ba las /
chos lugs bsgyur ba dang yi dam bsgyur ba sogs kyis chos spong du 'gro ba bka' dgongs 'grel gang nas kyang ma gsungs pas de 'dra chos spong du 'gyur snyam pa ni thos rgya chung ba'i rtags su gsal lo / /
! / /
khyung sprul rin po ches gsar 'dzugs g.yang sgam rang 'jags sam gnas spos gshegs gsol zhus na 'thus min gsungs pa re zhig thugs 'dod ltar mdzad pas chog /
kho bo'i shag tu yang o rgyan chen po'i snang brnyan dang /
rnying lugs kyi dpe cha mang du yod mus lags /
khyim lha rdo rje rab brtan ma dang rgyal chen thugs mi mthun pas ngan dogs yod @# / /
skad brjod 'dug pas 'khu ldog 'byung min zhes pa /
bon dang mu stegs pa'i lha dang /
ngo bo 'jig rten dregs pa lta bu yin na las / /
'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes kyi lha srung zhig yin phyin stong nyid mngon sum du rtogs pa'i 'phags pa rnams la nang mi mthun pa'i zhe sdang dang /
phrag dog nga rgyal sogs ci la srid /
de ltar yod par smra na mdo rgyud bstan bcos tshad ma dag dang 'gal /
yi dam dang srung ma rnams khro ba'i tshul mdzad pa yang nang phan tshun la min par /
bstan dgra sogs 'gro ba ma rungs pa rnams la khros shing /
de yang sems can de dang de dag rang rang la min par de dag la shin tu snying brtse bas de dag gi rgyud kyi bdag 'dzin dang gces 'dzin sogs nyon mongs rnams gzhom pa'i slad du khros pa yin no / /
des na 'jig rten phal pa rnams kyi rang rgyud kyi chags sdang phyogs ris sogs kyi skyon yi dam chos srung la sogs pa'i skyabs yul rnams la sbyar nas rnam rtog dgrar lang gis the tshom dang /
dogs pa mang du byas pas chos thams cad rtog pas phar btags kyi rten 'byung yin phyir rtog pas sgro btags pas de'i rjes 'brel gyi rten 'byung bslu ba med pas mi shis pa sogs 'byung ba yin la /
so so skye bo rnams 'di dang 'di lta bur 'khrul pa las kyang 'khrul pa a 'thas kyi rjes su zhugs pas mgo bo 'khor te srid pa'i 'khrul 'khor du 'phyan pa yin no / /
des na rgyal ba'i bstan pa dang lan cig mjal ba'i skabs 'dir rang zhen gyi phyogs lhung spangs te gzu bo'i blos bstan pa'i snying po btsal te gtan gyi 'dun ma rab tu sgrub par mdzad 'tshal / /

bul tog gnyer phan bde ye shes la gnang ba /
der bya bas mgon gyi snang brtan bzhengs rgyur tshang ma blo mos gros mthun byung ?ni| spyi sger tshang mar dge legs kyi sgo brgya yangs por 'byed pa'i skal bar smin nges shin tu legs shing /
ha chang phar 'gyangs su gyur na rnam dkar rlabs po che la bar chad 'byung nye bas lo nag lam brtsis par 'phral du sgrub ba legs la| gnas gong yang gser rin ji tsam 'phar ba tsam gyis bsod nams kyi tshogs je 'phel gyis /
bsod nams rin thang che chung gi khyad par gyis thob pa las /
mig sngar mdzes chos la bltos pa ma mchis pas /
de lugs rin gnas lam brtsegs par gtan bde'i tshogs gnyis bsgrub pa la shin tu rings par bya dgos / /

dge bshes smon lam rgya mtsho la gnang ba /
ji skad gsal bzhin dal 'byor gyi rten la snying po mchog lon pa ni cha chang zhing ma nor lam ? byang chub lam gyi rim pa nas ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin lam snga phyi'i go rim ma nor bar them skas bzhin rim pa ltar nyams len rdo rus thug par mdzad rgyu dang /
bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi nyams len chig sgril thog /
smon lam rnam dag gi mtshams sbyor shugs drag bcas mdzad na legs / /
! / /
gro mo dge bstan 'dzin bya mtsho la gnang ba /
yid bzhin nor bu 'bum las lhag pa'i dal brgyad 'byor bcu'i rten bzang 'di nyid ring por 'tsho ba'i thabs zab @# / /
gtsor bzung /
mnog chung tshe 'di'i don du gtan 'dun rlung la bskur ba'i snyigs dus kyi skye bo'i rjes su mi 'brang bar /
tshe 'di'i bde skyid thed la bor nas 'dod chung chog shes /
don nyung bya nyung 'phags pa'i rigs bzhi la gnas bzhin par /
byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i 'go bshes gnyen bsten tshul nas bzung /
dal 'byor dang /
mi rtag nas brtsams te zhi lhag gi bar gyi lam yongs rdzogs la thos bsam gyi nges pa 'dren cing /
thos don dmigs skor re la yang zla grangs zla grangs su dpyad sgom dang 'jog sgom gnad du bsnun te /
rtsol bcas rtsol med kyi myong ba zhig e thon 'bad na /
rtogs pa'i nyams myong gi rkang tshugs /
da gzod lam gyi sne zin bar 'gyur /
gzhan du mi tshe hril por ji tsam 'bad kyang rnam grangs gsog pa tsam las /
shes rgyud tha mal 'di bzhin gzhan du bsgyur bar mi nus pas de lugs nan tan du brtson par 'tshal / /
! / /
dom 'du dgon gyi 'dus tshogs la gnang ba /
mtha' 'khob kyi yul gru de lta bur blo bzang rgyal ba'i ring lugs lha ci /
rgyal bstan yang dag pa'i snang ba tsam yang shin tu phra bar lam log lam gol ltar snang log bshad kyis 'gengs pa'i rjes su skye bo phal cher zhugs te kun kyang lam log lam gol kho nar lceb pa'i yul dus de lta bur khyed cag bstan pa'i snying po blo bzang rgyal ba'i snyan brgyud dri ma med par thos bsam sgom gsum gyis 'jug tu yod pa ni shin tu e ma ho /
des na thams cad thugs mthun khrims gtsang ba'i ngos nas mdo sngags lam gyi rim par mang du thos pa dang tshul bzhin sgrub pa'i nyams myong rgyud thog tu 'gel zhing /
kun kyang gnas skabs kun tu bsre lhad med pa'i lta spyod gtsang ma dang /
'di snang gi phun tshogs la yid mi 'phrig par 'dod chung chog shes 'phags pa'i rigs bzhi la gnas pa sogs ji skad du /
phyi ru nyan thos spyod pas zhi zhing dul / /
nang du rim gnyis rnal 'byor gdeng dang ldan / /
zhes sogs ltar rang gzhan don gnyis spyi sgos bstan pa'i mig rgyan du 'gyur ba zhig kun gyis nan tan du slob pa 'tshal / /
! / /
bod sog bka' 'gyur bla ma 'jam dbyangs tshul khrims kyi dris lan /
bslab btus kyi btang bsrung dag spel bzhi ni /
lus lta bu la mtshon na /
snying rje'i bsam pa dag cing mgo sogs gtong ba la yang tshod ma spyin par gtong ba tsam las /
dka' ngal med pa'i dus su babs pa na lugs gtong ba dang /
de 'dra'i dus lam babs par lus ring du 'tsho phyir bsrung ba dang /
lus kyi kha nam tho bsam gos par byed pas lus dag pa dang /
tshe phyi ma yang rnam smin yon tan brgyad ldan dang theg mchog 'khor lo bzhi ldan gyi lus thob pa'i rgyu sgrub pa lus spel ba'o / /
longs spyod lta bur mtshon na /
mchog dman gyi zhing la gtong ba dang /
gzhan du chud mi zos pa'i bsrung ba dang /
log 'tsho ma 'dres pas longs spyod dag pa dang /
sbyin pas slar yang longs spyod 'phel bar byed pas longs spyod spel ba'o / /
de bzhin du dge rtsa la yang sbyar zhing /
de @# / /
rnams la phyin drug tshang tshul /
btang ba sbyin ba dang /
bsrung ba tshul khrims dang /
de dag nyams su len pa'i tshe yid mi 'khrug pa'i cha rnams bzod pa dang /
de ltar bsgrub pa la yid sro mi shi bar spro zhing 'dun pa'i cha rnams brtson 'grus dang /
de dag gi skabs yid rtse gcig pa'i cha rnams bsam gtan dang /
khyad par la so sor rtog pa'i cha rnams shes rab kyi nyams len la sbyar du rung /
spyir bslab btus rang du gsal bar yod mod /
'di rnams kyis kyang rags tsam shes par nus so / /
! / /
spom 'bor dge blo bzang nyi ma la gnang ba /
ji gsal bzhin /
dam sdom ma bsrung ba'i nyes dmigs sogs dran pa shin tu legs shing /
de yang sngon sor mo'i phreng ba can gyis mi dgu brgya dang dgu bcu go dgu bsang kyang sngar byas rnams nyes dmigs su rig nas 'gyod sdom tshul bzhin byas pas dgra bcom ba'i go 'phang thob tshul rnams bsams nas 'gyod sdom gyis bshags pa yun ring la shugs drag tu 'bad na las ngan rnams nges par byang ste zla ba sprin las grol ba ltar 'gyur bar bshes spring las gsungs pas /
tshe mjug 'dir bsags sbyang gtsor gyur gyis dal ba'i rten la snying po lon pa'i thabs mchog /
byang chub lam gyi rim par blo sbyangs nas bsrung sdom dang bsags sbyang gi gnad kyi nyams len rdo rus thug pa cis kyang mdzad na gtan gyi 'dun ma mchog 'grub par gdon mi za bas de don thugs su bsti bar 'tshal / /
! / /
sho mdo grwa sgom rin po cher gnang ba /
bla ma'i bka' la brtsi ba dang chos dwed du mi 'khyer ba'i bslab bya dgos gsungs pa /
bslab bya rgyas pa bri ma khom kyang mdor bsdus skyabs 'gro yang skabs brgyad bris te phul yod /
lar chos dred du mi 'gro ba'i rgyu'i gtso bo ni dal 'byor /
mi rtag pa /
sdug bsngal rnams bsgom pa nyid yin pas de dag la yang nas yang du dpyad sgom myong ba mthon bar byed pa nyid gtso bo yin cing /
bla ma'i bka' bzhin bsgrub pa'ang bshes gnyen bsten tshul gyi skor la dpyad sgom gyis myong ba 'don pa nyid gtso bo yin pas de lugs rgyud la bkri thabs la gang mkhas mdzad par zhu / /

brag g.yab 'jo khe bla ma ye shes dbang drag la gnang ba /
'jo khe bla ma rin po che nas dri ba mdzad pa'i dang po /
rnam par 'thag pa sdud pa'i mdo las /
sangs rgyas 'byung ba med par gzungs 'thob ces zer na chos spong ba yin no / /
gzungs thob pa'i thob pa ni yongs su dag pa ma yin no zhes zer na chos spong ba yin no / /
chos smra ba sgrub pa phun sum tshogs pa yin no / /
zhes zer na chos spong ba yin no / /
zhes gsungs pa'i don gang lags zhes phebs pa /
shing rta chen po'i gzhung la ma brten par mdo don rang dbang du 'grel ba bag tsha ba'i gnas kyang /
tshig don go tshod zhu na /
'jig rten na nyan thos dang /
rang sangs rgyas dang /
byang chub sems dpa' sogs ji snyed cig 'byung ba dang /
de dag gis gzungs thob pa sogs spangs rtogs kyi khyad par ji snyed mtha' dag sangs rgyas kho na la @# / /
brten nas thob dgos pas na sangs rgyas 'byung ba med par de dag yod ces smra na chos spong ba ste /
lung rtogs kyi chos la skur pa btabs par song ba'i don no / /
mdor na 'jig rten du sangs rgyas dkon mchog ma byung bar lung gi chos 'khor mi srid la /
de med pas rtags pa'i chos dkon mchog kyang 'jig rten du 'byung ba mi srid pas /
sangs rgyas ma byung bzhin du rtogs pa'i dam chos yod par smran nges par chos la skur pa btabs par 'gyur ro zhes pa'i don no / /
yang gzungs thob pa'i thob pa zhes pa ni gzungs thob pa'i thob bya la byed pa yin pas /
de lta bu'i thob bya yang yongs su dag pa ma yin zhes smra na nges par chos la skur pa btabs pa yin no / /
yang tshes smra ba sogs kyang de las ldog ste sbyar na go sla /
drib gnyis pa /
sngags lugs sems gsal rig tsam zhes pa /
gsal ba gang lags /
rig pa gang /
tsam sgras gang bcad so sor gsal ba zhu zhes phebs pa /
sems gsal rig tsam zhes ba 'di bzhin mdo lugs las /
sngags lugs la zur du mi 'dra ba'i khyad par gsungs pa med la /
mdo lags /
sems kyi kun rdzob pa'i ngo bo gsal ba /
stong pa /
rigs pa ste khyad chos gsum ldan /
phyag chen rtsa ba las /
mnyam gzhag ngo bo gang gis kyang / /
nas /
ci yang 'char ba'i hrig ge ba / /
zhes pa'i bar gsungs pa ltar sems kyi ngo bo kun rdzob pa de ni gang gis kyang ma sgrib pa'i dwangs shing gsal bas gsal ba /
de gzugs can gang du'ang ma grub pa'i stongs pa / /
yul ci yang 'char du rung ba'i hrig ge ba'i rig pa ste khyad chos gsum /

lan zhib tu spro na /
smyung gnas kyi sbyor ba gnyis pa'i thor thug skya rengs ma shar gong du btang na nyin snga ma'i mtshan mo'i cha yin pas phyi dro'i kha zas kyi nyes par 'gyur pas /
rgyal mchog bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i gsung las byung ba ltar skya rengs ma shar gong du thor thug gtong ba ni dgag bya dang nyes dmigs shin tu che zhing /
thor thug gtong mtshams gso sbyong gi sngon rjes gang du gtong yang bcas 'gal gyi nyes pa mi 'byung mod /
rang rang gi bla ma'i phyag bzhes kyi rjes su 'brangs na zhe gtsang bar gsungs pa ltar rang rang gi bla ma'i phyag bzhes kyi rjes su 'brangs na legs /
phal cher gyi phyag bzhes su nyin mo'i cha thog ma ni grub zin /
gso sbyong len ma ran pa'i bar der thor thug gtong mtshams khel bar mdzad pa min zhing /
de'i snga phyi'i mtshams ran pa zhig shin tu gal che bas /
de nyid zhib tu ngos 'dzin na /
skya rengs ni shar zin cing lag ris mi mthong ba'i dus tshun chod kyi bar der yin te /
skya rengs shar ba na nyin mo'i thog ma grub pas phyi dro'i kha zas kyi nyes pa mi 'byung zhing /
de 'phral lag ris mi mthong bas gso sbyong yang re zhig len mi ran pa'i phyir ro / /
des na skya rengs dang po 'char kha'i mdun rol phan ni snga nyin gyi mtshan mo dang /

sngon mnga' bdag nal pa can gyis bod 'bangs yongs kyi phyug dbul lan gsum cha snyoms par mdzad kyang /
da dung sngar mus nyid las mdzad thabs ma byung ba ltar ma zad /
padma bkod nas yar kong smad khul dang bcas par phal cher kla klo'i lugs su zhen cing /
chos lugs byed khul byas pa'ang lta log rdzun chos kho nas khengs pa'i ngan 'bras mthong chos su smin te padma bkod du'ang 'bras bu mi srid pa'i smyug mar 'bras bu smin cing /
de dag tshang ma srog chags byi bar gyur nas lo tog bcom pa sogs de ltar mi shis pa'i mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon sum du byung 'dug pa /
des na gtso bor rang rang dge bcu'i khrims dang /
blo bzang rgyal ba gnyis pa'i bstan par sri zhu bsgrub pa sogs tshul bzhin nus na bde skyid 'phel ba'i gnad che ba bcas zol med gsal 'debs su phul ba dgongs zab tu bsti bar 'tshal / /
! / /
phyogs mtha'i sprul sku zhig la stsal ba /
de ga bla brang sku sger du dgon gzhung spyi rdzas nas bzhes rgyu'i skor kya nom thugs blo khengs nges ma byung yang /
bla dgon dam gtsang la bsams nas mthun sgrig zhu mus yin tshul phebs pa de don shin tu legs shing /
da skabs dgon pa'i phugs kyi spyi don bstan 'gro'i bde rtsa'i gnas gzhi rlabs pa che 'dzugs pa'i @# / /
skabs 'dir drag zhan su 'dra nas kyang rang 'dod than 'khyer dgon spyir gnod rkyen cung zad tsam yang mi 'gro ba'i lhag bsam brtan gal che ba ma zad /
lam rim du ji gsungs ltar dge 'dun gyi spyi rdzas 'di rigs spyi mos dwang ba'i kun slong gis phul ba byung na las /
g.yo thabs kyis len pa khab skud tsam yang dmyal ba'i nye rgyur bsams te kho bos kyang shin tu 'dzem bya byed kyin yod lags na de gnas kyang ran tshod 'dod chung chog shes nan tar mdzad pa cis kyang gal che ba lags / /
! / /
dge rtse dpon bgres la gnang ba /
da lam ji ltar gsungs bzhin /
nyid nas 'di snang srid pa'i 'ching sgrog dpon gnas dgongs zhu gzhan 'gel zin pa dge sbyor gyi grogs su shin tu legs shing /
da cha 'di snang gi rnam g.yeng che bzhag chung ba shol gyis 'gro 'dug spyod lam gang spyi gang zhig bskyang bya'i dmigs rnam gyi thog tu bsgril gang thub nas /
sku na mtho ba sogs kyis thugs pham 'byung tshul gsal ba thugs med kyang /
ji skad du /
skra dkar gnyer ma lhags dus su'ang / /
thos pa bsag par bya ba ste / /
gang du thos mang 'gro 'gyur ba / /
der ni phung po 'gro mi 'gyur / /
ces sogs gsungs ba dang /
ma ti paN chen sogs sngon gyi dam pa mang pos kyang dgung grangs mthon por phebs zin pan gzhi nas chos la zhugs pas /
mthar mkhas grub gnyis ldan du gyur pa ji snyed cig byung ba bcas da phyin thugs brtson mdzad na gtan 'dun gyi snying po lon par nges| snying po len lugs kyang lam rim kho na la chig sgril dgos /
lam khrid skyong tshul gyi man ngag spom mda'i sbyin bdag las tshan par phul ba'i bslab bya zur bris kyis phul ba ltar nyams bzhes su bstar na mchog tu legs / /
! / /
chab mdo gnyer chen tshe dga' la stsal ba /
ji gsungs ltar nyid 'di snang la yid log ste gtan 'dun rtse gcig bsgrub sems bsten mus yod lugs de ltar du legs /
phyin chad kyang rje mid las /
zin pa med pa'i bya las de / /
bshol na zin pa 'khor ba'i gshis / /
zhes gsungs pa'i don ltar /
srid pa'i nyes phung chos brgyad dkar nag khra gsum gyi 'du long btsan chod du mdzad de /
rang gzhan lan ma phugs gtan du phan pa'i lha chos /
bstan pa'i snying po tshang lam nor ba'i lam gyi rim pa kho nar sang bya gnangs byas ma bslus par myur du gzhol na 'phral dang yun du mi slu ba'i lam 'bras rang rgyud la ring por mi thogs par 'byor bar nges pas de don thugs la thogs / /
! / /
dmag spyi'i drung zur skal bzang la stsal ba /
gang ltar 'jig rten 'di pa'i mkhyen gter 'jam pa'i dbyangs lta bu nyid la 'jig rten lugs kyi zhu bya ma dmigs shing /
'on kyang lugs zung bslab bya las /
dgra la ha cang sdang na rang la mtshungs / /
zhes pa ltar ha cang gyong thal du ma song ba zhig dang /
gzhi nas ji skad du /
gdong thug drag pos dgra bo 'dul dka' bas / /
sna tshogs thabs kyis 'dun ma rlabs kyis chod / /
ces pa ltar /
bdag gzhan mnyam pa rje ma nus kyang /
gnas @# / /

de lta na'ang /
tshe 'di yud tsam mdang gi rmi lam bzhin / /
tshong dus mgron po 'dzoms dang gyes pa bzhin / /
chos brgyad 'di yang byis pa'i rol rtsed bzhin / /
don chung las la snying por zhen pa nyid / /

gnas dus 'gro bsnyad /
'byor rgud /
rgyal pham gang la'ang thugs pham mi mdzad par gtso bor sku tshe gtan gyi 'dun mar ha cang pham nyes su ma shor ba zhig rten 'dir gal che bas de don mkhyen rab kyi klong du rol ba / /

rgya nag phyogs su rgya'i dge bsnyen nyu'u tshal mo kra ngal gnang ba /
de khul du dge ba shes rin po che ngag dbang rnam rgyal nas 'jam mgon ring lugs dri ma med pa'i srol bzang btsugs pa /
dge bsnyen gsar bu ba 'ga' nas bla ma'i gzugs brnyan gang byung la chos zhus te rang yul gyi bstan pa dri mas rnyog par byas yod tshod kyang| nyid sogs dge bsnyen rgan pa rnams nas col chung gang byung ma byas par rang lugs kyi grub mtha' dri ma med pa 'dzin bzhin bzhugs pa ngo mtshar che /
deng skabs 'jam dbyangs tsong kha pa'i bstan pa kho na ma gtogs /
sa skya| bka' brgyud /
rnying ma sogs thams cad kyi lta pa nor /
dbu ma thal 'gyur ba'i lta ba lta ci /
rang rgyud pa dang sems tsam pa'i lta ba tsam yang med par mu stegs pa dang /
hwa shang mahA ya na dang 'dra ba'i chad lta kho na bsgom /

bde stong /
'od gsal sgyu lus /
zung 'jug sogs kyi zab gnad kha phyogs tsam yang mi shes /
de dag la thar pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam ma nor ba med pas de 'dra la lo stong phrag tu sgrub pa nyams len byas kyang rtogs ba mi skye ba chu dkrogs nas mar 'dod pa dang 'dra bas snying po med /
de ltar na lta sgom spyod gsum /
mdo sngags gang gi thad la'ang 'khrul pa cung zad tsam yang med pa ni 'jam mgon tsong kha pa'i lugs bzang kho na yin /
des na khyed rang rnams dge ldan rang lugs gyi lta sgom dri ma med pa grub mtha' gzhan gyi bsre lhad med par 'dzin gal che bas de thugs su bzhag nas dge bshes rin po che las slar yang rang lugs kyi lta sgom spyod gsum nan tan du zhu zhing nyams su blangs na rang rang gi gtan gyi 'dun ma rab dang rtse mor son /
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa ngo ma dar zhing rgyas par 'gyur bas de lugs thugs dgongs su bsti ba dang /
yi ge 'di don rnams rgya yig tu bsgyur nas dge bsnyen gzhan rnams la'ang sgrog par 'tshal / / / /

deng dus 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir rgya gar /

rigs mtho ba /
gzugs bzang ba sogs tshe 'di'i bde skyid phun sum tshogs pa shin tu mang po yod kyang /
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa lam zhugs pas tshe 'di la bde skyid che ba tsam las /
phyi mar skye ba 'bum phrag mang bor ngan song gsum las thar dus med par sdug bsngal dpag med myong dgos pa red /
rang re'i dpon po chen po li'u cun krang 'di nyid chos lugs nang pa sangs rgyas pa la zhugs /
de'i nang nas kyang bstan pa'i snying po 'jam dpal dbyangs tsong kha pa'i bstan pa la zhugs par mdzad pas /
dpon mo chen mo nyid kyang 'jam mgon tsong kha pa'i bstan pa dang mjal /
de'i chos lugs mdzad pa 'di bsod nams shin tu che| las dang skal ba shin tu bzang /
sgrub pa rtse gcig tu ma nus pas tshe 'di la thar pa thob ba zhig ma thub kyang /
skye ba phyi mar ha cang thag ring min bar thar pa dang sangs rgyas thob pa'i sa bon khyad par can rgyud la bzhag nges red /
des na phyin chad kyang tshe phyi ma la rang gcig pu 'jig rten pha rol tu 'gro ba'i skabs su phan pa ni chos kho na yin /
chos lugs thams cad kyi mchog /
rgyal po lta bu ni tsong kha pa'i lugs gcig pu yin pas 'di rang gis nyams su gang lon dang /
rang gis nyams len chen po ma thub kyang rang gi yul du dar gang thub mdzod dang rang dang gzhan gyi skye ba 'bum phrag mang po'i don 'grub /
ngan song gi sgo bcad /
mtho ris dang thar pa'i sgo phye /
sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang gi rtsa ba bcugs pa yin pas rang gzhan gnyis ka la phan pa'i don 'di las lhag pa med pas nan tan thugs kyi dkyil du chongs / /

sa stag lor rgya'i dpon chen lu'u cun krang la gnang ba /
deng gi dus sa chen po'i khyon du 'khod pa'i rgyal po /
rgyal phran phal cher kla klo'i chos lugs la mchog tu 'khrul te sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i bdud rtsi las rgyab kyis phyogs nas rang nyid sde 'bangs dang bcas par ngan song gi sgo yangs por phye ba'i dus 'dir /
dpon po chen po khyod nyid ni sngon gyi smon lam dang bsod nams kyi mthu dpung btsan pos sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i snying po 'jam mgon tsong kha pa chen po'i ring lugs kho na spyi bo'i gtsug tu bkur /
thugs kyi mthil du bzung ste rang gi yul sogs zhing chen du mar khyab gdal du dar par mdzad pas rang gzhan skye 'gro khri phrag nas khri phrag mang po'i rgyud la bstan pa dri ma med pas thar pa'i sa bon bskrun te rnam grol gyi lam yangs por mdzad pa'i mdzad pa bzang po 'di la kho bos bsam bzhin bsam bzhin dang 'bro dang yi rang dpag tu med pa rgya mtsho'i rba rlabs mkha' la 'phyur ba ltar thob pa bka' drin shin tu che /
da dung yang sa steng 'di na mu stegs /
ye shu /
mu sul man /
kong tse /
bon sogs lugs mang po dar ba rang rang gi lugs de mchog tu ba rloms kyang /
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa kho na ma gtogs gzhan tshang mar thar pa'i lam med /
nyon mongs sna gcig kyang spong ba'i nus pa med /
dus yun ring por dka' thub drag pos @# / /
nyams su blangs kyang ngan song gi sgo 'byed pa las 'bras bu bzang po ci yang thob mi nus /
lam ma yin pa lam du ston pa'i bslu ba'i tshig kho na yin /
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa ni de las ldog ste /
thar pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i go 'phang bde blag tu ster /
'khor ba dang ngan song gi skye sgo gcod /
nyon mongs pa brgyad khri bzhi stong bag chags dang bcas pa rtsa ba nas spong bar nus /
dka' spyad snying rus ha cang chen po mi dgos par lam bde ba nas 'bras bu bde ba thob /
bden pa'i bka' nam yang bslu ba med pa kho na yin pas /
des na rang re rnams skye ba gtan gyi don bzang po zhig sgrub na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa kho na la 'jug dgos /
bstan pa de la grub mtha' smra ba bzhi yod kyang rtag chad kyi g.yangs dang bral ba'i stong pa nyid ma nor ba rgyal ba'i dgongs pa mthar thug ji bzhin du rtogs pa ni dbu ma thal 'gyur ba kho na yin /

bka' brgyud /
sa skya| dge lugs sogs grub mtha' mi 'dra ba mang yang /

lta ba tsam du ma zad /
sgom pa rnam dag bying rmugs dang bral ba dang /
spyod pa rnam dag 'dul ba ltar sgrub pa ste lta sgom spyod gsum dang /
sangs rgyas kyi gsung rab yongs su rdzogs pa lam gyi rim pa gcig tu bsgril nas 'khyer shes pa sogs ri bo dge lugs pa kho na las med pas /
des na 'jam mgon tsong kha pa'i lugs dpal mnyam med ri bo dge ldan pa'i bstan pa 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa thams cad kyi snying po rgyal mtshan gyi tog ltar gyur pa yin pas 'di nyid rang gis 'dzin cing gzhan la spel ba ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rlabs po che mchog tu gyur pa yin pas na /
dpon po chen po khyod kyis sngon chad ji ltar mdzad pa ltar rgya nag gi zhing chen por dar zhing rgyas pa'i thabs gang la ci drag dang /
khams kyi yul gru rnams su yang nyams pa sor chung /
mi nyams gong 'phel gyi thabs tshul bskyang 'os sogs gang ci nas ri bo dge ldan pa'i bstan pa'i thugs khur 'khyer ba'i rgyal sras kyi spyod pa bzang po sngar bzhin lhod med bka' drin stsol ba / /

yangs yos lor lu'u cun krang la 'bul gnang mdzad pa /
! 'jam gling phyi nang gi grub mtha' spyi'i gnas tshul drang por brjod pa bzhugs /

'byed pa red /
bon po zhes pa 'di yang phyi rol mu stegs pa'i lugs dang khyad med /

kod tse'i lugs kyang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa ma yin pas gnas skabs kyi bde thabs cam las thar pa med /
lugs 'di rnams tshang ma sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa las phyi rol tu gyur pa yin pas 'tshang rgyab phar bzhag /
thar pa tsam thob pa'i lam gtan nas med /
'di rnams kyi chos byas nas thar pa thob pa gcig kyang ston rgyu med /

sangs rgyas kyi chos lugs la'ang /
bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa thugs rje can gyis /
dang po nyid nas zab mo stong nyid kyi mthar thug bstan na gdul bya'i blo la mi chud pas /
dper na byis pa rnams la yi ge ka kha nas rim gyis slob pa ltar thog mar sla ba'i chos bstan te gang zag gi bdag med rags pa tsam ston pa'i bye brag smra ba'i grub mtha' bstan /
de nas de las cung bzang tsam gyi mdo sde pa'i grub mtha' bstan /
de nas de las cung bzang ba chos kyi bdag med rags pa tsam ston pa'i sems tsam pa bstan /
'di thang san bla mas rgya nag gi yul du dar rgyas mdzad /
de nas lta ba'i mthar thug bdag med phra mo ston pa'i dbu ma'i grub mtha' bstan cing /
de la'ang rgya gar gyi slob dpon legs ldan 'byed dang zhi 'tsho sogs kyis dbu ma'i grub mtha' la zhugs kyang /
stong nyid shin tu phra bas sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa mthar thug lon ma thub pas dbu ma 'bring tsam yin /
de dag la dbu ma rang rgyud pa zer /
yang rgya gar gyi slob dpon sangs rgyas bskyangs dang zla ba grags pas sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa mthar thug mgon po klu sgrub kyis srol phyes pa ma nor bar gting phyin par rtogs /
de la dbu ma thal 'gyur ba zer /
thar pa dang sangs rgyas thob byed kyi lam la thabs kyi cha dang shes rab kyi cha gnyis yod pas /
rang rgyud pa man chad kyi nang pa'i grub mtha' smra ba rnams kyis thabs kyi lam rnams ma nor ba rnyed kyang /
shes rab kyi cha'i lta ba mthar thug rtogs ma thub pas stong pa nyid cha 'dra tsam las ngo ma de rtogs ma thub /
des na stong nyid phra mo ma nor ba sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa mthar thug rtogs pa dbu ma thal 'gyur ba kho na yin /
thal 'gyur ba'i lugs la ma zhugs na stong nyid ngo ma rtogs pa gcig kyang med /
de med pas thar pa thob pa med /

zab cing myur ba med /

ha cang zab cing phrabs rjes 'jug tshos mkhas grub gong ma rnams kyi dgongs pa'i phugs rtogs ma thub par lta ba nor /

sgom pa /

dgongs gter /

'di dag gi rjes su 'brangs te zhi khro'i skor mang du byung zhes snang /

kaHthog dang /
ze chen dgon sogs yod 'dug /
de dag tu mdo sgyu sems gsum sogs chos kyi snying po rnams ni ka dag gdod ma'i klong du thim nas ring zhig lon pas /
da lta'i rnying ma ba rnams las byang gyer ba dang /
tshogs 'khor gyi yo lang dang /
mnan sreg 'phang gsum sogs las sbyor gyi gzugs brnyan la snying por byed pa tsam mo / /
zhes dang /
si tu'i skye brgyud chos kyi nyin byed bya bas khams sde dger dpal spungs chos sde btab /
dus phyis tha snyad rig gnas la 'di las mkhas pa ma byung ba lta bu snang /
gsar 'gyur dang 'gyur bcos mdzad pa dang /
rig gnas kyi rtsom pa'ang shin tu mang /
'on kyang de'i rnam thar na si tu dang po dbu ma'i lta ba 'dzin pa la /

mchod rten bya rung kha shor gyi drung du phyin chad dbu ma'i lta ba dor nas gzhan stong gi lta ba 'dzin par dam bcas so / /

zhes dang /
yang de nyid las /
bod kyi grub mtha' ba phal mo che zhig gis /

de dag ni /
mdo sde rgyan las /
'di na dang por thos la brten nas tshul bzhin yid la byed pa 'byung / /

dge ldan pa'i ring lugs 'di la /
mdo sde'i sde @# / /
snod la thos bsam bgyis te theg pa gong 'og gi bslab pa gsum ka gtan la pab /
'dul ba'i sde snod la thos bsam bgyis te tshul khrims dan ting nge 'dzin gnyis sgrub bar byed /
mngon pa'i sde snod la thos bsam bgyis te chos rnams kyi mtshan nyid ma nor bar rig pa'i shes rab bskyed nas shes rab kyi bslab pa sgrub par byed cing mngon sum du thob par byed /
khyad par du theg chen gyi sde snod las byang chub kyi sems dang /
sa dang pha rol tu phyin pa'i spyod pa rgya chen po dang /
bdag med phra mo rigs pa'i rnam grangs mtha' yas pa'i sgo nas bstan pa rnams thos bsam sgom ba'i gtso bor byed pa yin pas /
lugs mchog tu gyur pa 'di nyid la bstan pa spyi dang khyad par du theg chen gyi bstan par 'jog byed kyi mtshan nyid yongs su rdzogs pa dang ldan pa yin no / /
'jog byed kyi chos de la gsang sngags ma tshang ngo snyam na /
gsang sngags spyi ni mdo sde'i sde snod du 'du ba dbung bzang gi rgyud dang rgya gar paN chen gyis gsungs la /

dbyibs kyi gzugs /
snang ba'i gzugs sogs dang /
'du shes la rkang med rkang mang rkang bzhi'i 'du shes sogs bshad pa lta bu dang /

bskyed rdzogs kyi skabs su nga rgyal dang gsal snang gi sgo nas thun mong ma yin pa'i ting nge 'dzin sgrub tshul ston pa rnams mdo sde dang /

de gsum gyi sgo nas grub mtha' gzhan thams cad las dge lugs pa khyad par du 'phags ba yin te /
de yang lta ba'i sgo nas khyad par du 'phags tshul ni /
bod snga rabs pa kha cig stong pa nyid kyi don ci yang med pa zhig tu bzung nas dge mi dge las 'bras sogs gtan med du 'dod pa'i chad lta ngan pa la lta ba mchog tu 'dzin par byed /
'di ni 'thad pa ma yin te /
mu stegs kyi tha chad rgyang 'phen pa la rtog ge ba dang snyoms 'jug pa gnyis yod pa'i nang tshan snyoms 'jug ba 'ga' zhig gis skye ba brgya tshun chad sogs kyi las rgyu 'bras khas len kyang thar pa khas mi len la /
rtog ge bas las 'bras dang thar pa med mnyam du 'dod pa yin gyi las 'bras gtan med du bzung nas thar lam sgrub pa'i grub mtha' phyi nang gi rigs smra sus kyang khas mi len pas so / /
yang 'ga' zhig stong pa nyid bden grub yin cing /
de kun rdzob pa'i chos gzhan gyis stong pa'i gzhan stong ni gnas lugs mthar thug yin no zhes zer /

lan re /

de yang 'thad pa ma yin te /
yod med dang /
rtag mi rtag dang| gcig tha dad sogs ni rnam bcad yongs gcod kyi sgo nas phan tshun spangs te 'gal bar rgya gar paN chen gyi lung rigs kyis grub cing /

ma 'ongs ba'i sdun me bsu /

de yang 'thad pa ma yin te /
gang yang yid la ma byas par bsdad pas gang yang mi mkhyen pa med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rgyud la skye na mi mthun pa'i rgyu las mi mthun pa'i 'bras bu 'byung bas thams cad las thams cad skye bar 'gyur ro / /
rgyas par ni rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i legs bshad lam rim dang /
rtsa 'jug gi rnam bshad /
sras kyi thu bos mdzad pa'i stong thun skal bzang mig 'byed dang /
lta khrid lta ngan mun sel sogs las 'byung ba ltar ro / /
des na snga rabs pa de dag gis don dam dpyod byed kyi rigs pas dpyad pa na dgag bya ma lus pa khegs pa dang /
bkag pa'i shul du las 'bras bya byed sogs bsnyon med du 'jog shes pa'i gnyis tshogs de 'jog ma shes pas dman la /
nges don 'grel par rgyal ba rang nyid kyis lung bstan pa'i dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub yab sras kyi gzhung gi rjes su 'brangs te /
'khor 'das kyi chos thams cad rang rang gi gdags gzhi'i ngos nas don dam par grub pa rdul tsam yang mi dmigs kyang gdags gzhi'i steng du ming dang rtog pas phar bzhag tsam de tha snyad du tshad mas grub la /
chos rnams rang rang gi ngo bos stong pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis tha snyad du chos de dang der grub cing bya byed sogs 'thad ldan du 'jog shes pas /

la las /
rnam rtog ma rig chen po ste / /
'khor ba'i rgya mtshor ltung bar byed / /
ces gsungs pas rnam rtog ma rig pa yin zer /
la las rnam rtog chos sku yin zer /
'ga' zhig gis yid ma 'phros par sa le hrig ge gnas ba'i tshe sangs rgyas sam myang 'das yin /
cung zad gcig 'phros pa nas sems can nam 'khor ba yin ces zer /
kha cig mun khung du lus kyi byed bcing dang mig gi lta stangs gcun nas sems ci yang yid la mi byed par bzhag pa'i tshe du sogs kyi nyams snang za zi gang shar thams cad chos sku dang ngo bo nyid sku yin pas so so skye bos kyang chos sku mngon sum du mthong zhes zer /
kha cig de dag chos sku yongs rdzogs mthong ba min gyi chos sku'i cha shas tsam zhig mthong ba yin ces zer /
kha cig de dag chos sku ma yin kyang myur du chos sku mthong bar 'gyur ba'i snga ltas su gyur pa'i lam rtags yin ces zer /
kha cig sems 'khrul ba'i 'khrul snang ban bun yin pas snying po ci yang med ces zer /
kha cig de dag 'dus byas yin ces zer| kha cig de dag 'dus ma byas yin ces zer ba sogs sgom gyi ngo bo la 'khrul ba mang du smra bar byed do / /
de dag kyang 'thad pa ma yin te /
rnam rtog thams cad spang bya yin na stong nyid rtogs pa'i rigs shes rjes dpag kyang spong dgos la /

sangs rgyas la spangs rtogs nyams pa mi srid pas lnga ba mi 'thad /

sgom thams @# / /

las dang @# / /
po pas ting nge 'dzin gsar du sgrub pa'i tshe gnas cha tsam gyis mi chog par gsal ba'i ngar dang ldan pa dgos tshul sogs shing rta chen po'i gzhung gi dgongs pa ji lta ba bzhin du phyin ci ma log par gtan la phab pa yin pas rnam pa thams cad du 'khrul pa dang bral ba yin no / /
de nyid kyi phyir lam rim gyi zhi gnas gsungs pa'i mjug tu /
mdo dang dgongs 'grel bstan bcos chen mo las / /
legs gsungs ting 'dzin bsgrub pa'i rim pa ni / /
rjod byed brling bas blo gros chung rnams kyis / /
ji bzhin ma rtogs rang gi blo yi skyon / /
gzhan la bsgos pas gzhung bzang de dag la / /
mi rtog skyong ba'i gdams pa med snyam nas / /
yod pa'i gzhung dum btsal med pa'i sar / /
'bad pa du mas tshol zhing rnyed par sems / /
de 'dras phyi rol pa dang nad pa yi / /
ting 'dzin rnams kyang phyed par mi 'gyur na / /
theg pa mchog dang theg pa dman pa dang / /
rdo rje theg dang pha rol phyin pa yi / /
ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par gang yin pa /
ji bzhin phyed par 'gyur ba smos ci dgos / /
tshul de mthong nas gzhung lugs chen mo yi / /
ting 'dzin skyong tshul go sla'i ngag gis bshad / /
gzhung lugs che la lo mang sbyangs pa yi / /
grogs dag rang gi nor bu rin po che / /
dor nas gzhan gyi mching bu ma len par / /
rang la rin chen yod pa mkhyen par mdzod / /
khyod kyis sbyangs pa'i gzhung las gdams pa'i don / /
logs su med par gzigs nas thub dbang gis / /
mang du thos pa nags na bde'o zhes / /
gsungs pa de yi don la'ang dpyod par rigs / /
zhes gzhung lugs mang du thos pa rnams dang /
ci yang mi rtog 'jog pa'i zhi gnas lam / /
dang por sgrub pa'i tshul dang grub pa'i tshad / /
legs par dmigs phyed go ba ma rnyed kyang / /
snying rus tsam la re ba'i bsam gtan pa / /
de dag gis kyang da dung mkhas pa la / /
brten nas skyong tshul ji bzhin shes par mdzod / /
de lta min na rgyal ba'i bstan pa la / /
re zhig ngal 'tsho byas na gnod pa chung / /
zhes blun sgom tsam gyis chog shes bgyid pa rnams la thugs brtse bas bslab bya'ang 'doms par mdzad pa yin no / /
de lta na ri bo dge ldan pa'i ring lugs 'di nyid lhag pa ting nge 'dzin gyi yon tan gyi sgo nas kyang gzhan las khyad par 'phags pa 'grub bo / /
spyod pa'i sgo nas kyang khyad par du 'phags te /
bod snga ma phal cher 'di skad du /
myos 'gyur gyi btung ba dang /
phyi dro'i kha zas spong ba sogs 'dul ba las gsungs pa ni theg pa 'og ma dman pa la mos pa dag gi dbang du byas pa yin gyi /

sku gdung rin po che ril por bzhugs rgyu'i rigs la nang du rul sungs mi 'jug ched rtsa bshal chu bshal lta bu 'bul rgyur /

de thog tshwa chu gang nus phul te gdung tshwa'i nang bzhugs su gsol bas dngul chu rnams sku'i gsang sgo nas dri ma dang chabs cig babs pa slar yang dngul chu gsar pa 'bul zhing gdung tshwa brje ba sogs yang yang skam thag mchod bar du bya /
sku'i mchan khung dang bla'i khug sogs su'ang tshwa zhib cung zad 'bul ba yang yang brje dgos /
zhugs 'bul gyi rigs la me bzhes khyang sku'i nang du si la khyon che 'bul yang /
ril por bzhugs rgyu'i rigs la si la phul na des 'gags nas dngul chu dang tshwa chu sogs 'bul lam mi rnyed pas sku gdung chud zos su 'gro ba'ang shin tu mang pas si la sogs gtan nas 'bul mi nyan /
de min gdung khrus 'bul lugs sogs rin chen sgron ma ltar mdzad na 'thus pa bcas dbyings rol zhu / /
! / /
mtha' 'khob spo bo'i yul du stsal ba'i dur khrod bzo lugs kyi zin bris /
dur khrod bzo lugs rang phyogs kyi yig cha khungs dag gang yang ma mthong zhing /
khams phyogs dpal 'bar sprul sku rin po che sogs nas dgon sde sogs su dur khrod gsar pa mang du bzo gnang mdzad 'dug cing /
de yang 'ga' zhig bde mchog dang /
'ga' zhig rnal 'byor ma sogs kyi dkyil 'khor yin tshul gsungs snang ba ji ltar mdzad zhib tu rtsad gcod bgyis par /
dur 'jog sa'i 'og mi tshad las lhag tsam sa brus pa'i sding du lha gang gi dkyil 'khor du byed pa de'i ras bris dang sku gsung thugs kyi dkyil 'khor mchod gtor dang bcas pa legs par bsgrigs nas /
bla ma dang dge 'dun sogs kyis bdag mdun gyi bskyed chog legs par byas /
nyer bsdu ma byas par bzhag nas mtha' skor dang steng 'og sogs nas nyams skyon zhig ral du mi 'gyur ba'i sgrom sogs legs par bzos pa'i steng du thog phubs /
de'i steng du sa rdo rim bkabs kyis /
khar phung po 'jog sa'i rdo gcal sogs btings nas de la dkyil 'khor de dang de'i tha snyad byed cing /
ming yang dur khrod mi zer bar gtan chags zer ba sogs mdzad 'dug pa /
phung po de dkyil 'khor nyer bsdu ma byas pa de'i steng du gtor ba /
dkyil 'khor de yi lha tshogs kyi spyan sngar 'grem bzhin tshogs su phul ba lta bu yin nyams che ba yod skad dang /
bla ma chen pos mdzad pa la khungs rnam dag cig yod pa shin tu los dgos kyang /
rang phyogs kyi mkhas pa rnams kyis de la dgag pa @# / /
mdzad pa yang 'ga' shas snang zhing /
dkyil 'khor lta ci smos te lha'i mtshan ma dang dman ma sogs la'ang 'go ma yug phra mo tsam yang mi nus na /
dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs dngos su bshams pa nyer bsdu tsam yang ma byas pa'i steng du ro tha mal pa 'jog pa phan yon las nyes dmigs lci bar mi 'gyur ram zhes gsungs mkhan mang du snang ba thugs shin tu bden par 'dra ba ma zad /
rang re bod kyi pha bong kha dang /
se 'bras kyi dur khrod rnams la'ang 'og tu de 'dra yod ba mi snang bas /
de 'dra re zhig rung mi rung kha tshon gcod dka' bas btang snyoms su bzhag nas /
spyir dur khrod kyi skad dod sham sha na zhes pa ro'i spyod lam rnam bzhi byed pa dang /
mgo rus dang byin pa'i rus pa sogs mang du 'thor ba mi'i phung po mang du bskyal ba'i gnas shig la dur khrod ces ming btags pa tsam du mngon la /
'on kyang phung po gang du gtor ba'i gnas der gshin gyi bla de chags shing /
bla de dar gud la brten nas rjes 'jug gson po rnams la'ang phan gnod kyi khyad par 'byung bas /
de 'dra'i sa des bkra bzang ba zhig nges par gal che zhing /
sa sde skyes bu dam pas byin gyis brlabs shing dpa' bo mkha' 'gro dngos su 'du ba'i gnas dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi bkod pa rang bzhin gyis chags pa'am /
rnal 'byor pa chen pos sngags dang ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par gyis gsar du bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi gnas gzhi lta bu byin rlabs can zhig yin na gshin bo la'ang nges bar phan zhing| sngon gyi dur khrod rnying pa rnams la'ang lha'i dkyil 'khor gyi sgras btags pa 'ga' re snang ba yang de 'dra yin tshod bcas /
des na dur khrod bzo tshul gyi yig cha khungs btsun sngar mig lam du ma son zhing /
da lam dpe mang blta rtog byed pa ma 'grub pas khungs dang bcas 'di zhes zhu rgyu ma mchis kyang /
bka' do ma ldog tsam rang gi bsam tshod ltar zhu na /
dang pos dpyad legs pa gal che bas /
rgyas par na jo bo rjes mdzad pa'i sa dpyad dang /
bai dkar gyis dpyad sogs las gsungs pa'i dur gyis bkra legs pa spyi dang /
mdor nas gzhi bag dro zhing byin chags pa /
sa der slebs pa tsam gyis bag phebs sdod nyams spro ba /
der nyal nas bltas pas mthong sar bkra ngan pa med pa de 'dra zhig legs par btsal /
de 'dra'i sa der sngags rim chen mo dang dkyil chog sogs las byung ba ltar gyis brtag pa /
bslang ba /
sbyang ba /
bzung ba /
byin gyis brlab pa bcas bya zhing /
gzhan yang gzhi der mi shis pa bsal ba'i phyir zhi ba'i sbyin sreg tshar kha shas dang /
'dul lugs kyi rab gnas dang sa gzhi byin rlabs gso sbyong yin pas /
dge slong tshul khrims rnam dag tshogs pa nas gso sbyong yang bya /
dngos gzhi lha gang gi dkyil 'khor bya ba rang rang gi 'dod mos chog kyang /
rgyud sde 'og ma gsum dang /
bla med gsang 'dus sogs la dur khrod med pas de dag ma yin pa'i bde kyai /
'jigs byed sogs gshed skor /
rnal 'byor ma sogs phag mo'i @# / /
rigs lta bu dur khrod yod pa'i bla med kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rigs gang rung zhig byas na legs shing /
de yang sa de lha de dag gi gnas ri yin pa sogs sngon nas gsal kha yod rigs la dur khrod kyang de dang de'i dkyil 'khor byas na legs shing /
de rigs med pa dang sbyir btang dur khrod skyong ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo bcom ldan 'das dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nyid yin pas dur khrod kyang bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor du byas na byin che 'brel chags la /
ji ltar bya ba'i tshul ni /
gong du brjod pa'i gzhan lugs de ltar 'og tu dkyil 'khor bsgrig ba sogs mi bya bar /
rnal 'byor pa tshad ldan ting nge 'dzin brtan po dang ldan pa ji ltar 'dus pa dag gzhi der 'tshogs nas bdag bskyed btang /
mdun bskyed sgrub gzhi ras bris dang rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor sogs med par /
bsam gtan gyi dkyil 'khor ltar gzhi de nyid du rten dang brten pa'i dkyil 'khor gtso bo nas dur khrod kyi bar legs par gsal gang bcing| ye shes ba bstim pa sogs nas gtang rag gi mchod bstod bar gyi dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod rgyas par btang /
mdun bskyed kyi rten dang brten pa ma bsdus par gnas gzhi de nyid du bkra lam mer bzhugs pa la der gung po 'dor ba sogs 'brel tshad don ldan gyi 'phrin las bcol zhing gsol 'debs byed /
de nas smon lam shis brjod sogs legs par bya /
de lta bu'i sgrub mchod bdun gcig /
gnyis /
gsum sogs gang nus bya ba ni dngos gzhi'i rim pa'o / /
rjes su yang rnal 'byor pa rtogs pa dang ldan pa dang /
bdag pas gzhan gces kyi byang sems 'byongs pa dang /
'dul 'dzin 'tshul khrims rnam par dag pa sogs gang zag khyad par can lta spyod rnam dag byon tshad la gzhi der rang rang gi thugs dam skyong ba dang bden tshig sogs zhu zhing /
lta sgom dang ldan pa'i gcod pa nus ldan dag nas kyang gzhi der lus spyin yang yang bya /
grub na g.yas g.yon du byang chub mtshod rten lta bur gzungs 'bul gyi yi ge khungs ldan dag las gsungs pa'i gzungs spyi dang /
lhag par ngan song sbyong pa'i gzungs sde rnams gang mang phul ba legs par bzhengs /
de 'dra'i dur khrod du thog mar 'gri ma rgyu'i phung po yang bai dkar gshin rtsis kyi le'u nas gsungs pa'i dur du 'jog mi nyan ba'i rigs ma yin pa smos ci /
rgyun du yang mdze dang grir shi ba sogs kyi ro ma yin par rigs bzang ba dang /
rgyud 'jam pa /
tshul khrims gtsang ba sogs kyi phung po 'jog cing /
de yang dpal ldan 'khor lo sdom ba'i tshogs kyi 'khor kho dang bcas te 'bul ba lta bu yi dam gyi dkyil 'khor gang yin pa de'i tshogs su bsngo zhing 'bul /
yang na gcod pa bzang pos gcod tshogs su bsngo ba sogs sha chen bam gyi tshogs 'khor bya /
yul der bya rgod gtan nas med na yul gzhan nas rim gyis 'khrid pa'i thangs la brtson /
gzhan yang gzhi der mtshan brjod dang /
gzungs 'dus sogs gzungs mdo khyad par can mang du sgrog pa sogs bya /
'di dag ni rang gi bsam tshod dang bstun nas legs @# / /
par sbyar ba yin la /
slar dpe khungs dag 'dra rnyed na go bsdur zhing /
gal te ma rnyed kyang 'di la legs par yid rton chog pa yod do / /
'di ni bshad sgra'i rtsis dpon sku ngo dpal 'byor bsod nams rab brtan la gnang ba'o / /
! gtsang bkras lhun grwa rigs dkon mchog ye shes la stsal ba /
ji gsal /
nyid sku khams bde min de dag gzhi rtsa dge sbyor gyi lhong yin nges kyang /
de gcig pu tsam min par 'byung ba 'khrungs pa'i nad kyi skyon yang cung zad yod 'dra bas sman bcos sogs kyang nan tan mdzad na legs /
dge sbyor gyi lhong la legs sel bogs 'don gyi rgyal po ni bla ma'i rnal 'byor nyid yin pas /
mchod tshogs bzang po dang bcas te rkyen ngan zhi zhing dge sbyor la bogs thon pa'i gsol 'debs shugs drag yang yang mdzad gal che zhing /
lte ba'i rlung snying gar zhugs pa de dag 'og rlung shugs che 'then drags pa'i rlung gegs yin phyir re zhig 'og rlung gtan nas mi 'then bar steng rlung mnan pa'i dmigs pa kho na gtso 'don dang /
phar tsam bar ma ning ha 'don kyang ma mdzad pa legs /
da lta'i nad 'di dang 'dres te snying rlung khrag rlung sogs kyi nad gzhi yod med rtog dpyod kyis yod na de'i gnyen po'i sman zab tu bsten dgos /
yang ji gsungs /
sems kyi 'gyu ba snang ba sna tshogs shar ba de rnams nyams kyi 'char sgo rang yin par /
rje mid las kyang /
sems kyi 'char sgo 'di nyi zer gyi rdul bas kyang mang ba zhig gda' ste /
zhes sogs gsungs pa ltar rnal 'byor pa la nyams mang ba dge sbyor byas pa'i rtags yin zhing /
'on kyang de la dgag sgrub spang blang re dogs gang yang mi bya bar chos nyid zab mo stong pa nyid kyi dad du bskyur te 'jog pa gnad che /
'di dag la lhong tshad tshar tshad sogs kyis sems mi bde ba dang /
lus kyi na tsha| gzhan gyi rkyen ngan gyis gtses pa /
'jigs skrag gi snang ba che ba sogs 'byung ba 'di dag lam du ma lhongs na srog gi bar chad du yang 'gyur ba srid cing /
lam du lhongs na de dag chod pa'i rjes su nyams rtogs bzang po skye bas na 'di dag gi skabs lhong dang rkyen gyi dbang du ma song ba'i tshar lhong chod gsum sgrig thabs rang lugs gcod kyi gzhung chen mo rnams su gsungs yod pa de dag la'ang zhib tu rtog zhib mdzod /
gzhan yang zhu mi shes pa'i zhu rgyu mang po 'dug gsungs pa de dag kyang bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi khongs nas dogs pa gcod thabs dang /
de khul dka' chen rin po che sogs nyams myong can gyi rigs la'ang 'dri gtug mdzad thog /
dge sbyor la ha cang brtson ches pa dang sems nang du ha cang bsdus drags pa sogs kyi skyon du mi 'gyur pa'i phyer skabs su khams gseng ba dang /
ngal bso bag yangs bya ba sogs kyang brtson 'grus kyi nyams len dor ba'i stobs su ji ltar gsungs pa ltar dang /
bga' gdams gong mtshos dge sbyor thang lhod ran par yun bsrings pa'i rnam thar ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin phyag len du bstar mdzod / /

spyan seng blo bzang mkhas grub la gnang ba /
nyid kyi 'phrin yig tu gsal bzhin /
mi tshangs spyod kyi nyes bas gos par nyes ba la nyes par @# / /
mthong bas gnong 'gyod drag pos bshags shing 'dag thabs lhur len pa ni /
mkhas pa'i sdig pa lci yang yang / /
zhes pa ltar ring por mi thogs par sdig ltung las ldang bar nus nges shin tu legs /
'on kyang sdig sgrib sbyong thabs sems khrid las lhag pa med tshul dang /
rnam rtog sems su ngo sprad nas sdig pa med tshul /
tshogs drug rang grol /
gnas 'gyu rig gsum /
shar grol dus mnyam /
sku lnga sku bzhi sku gsum sems su ngo sprod tshul sogs brtse ba chen pos stsal du gsol /
zhes gsungs pa 'di dag rnying ma dang rdzogs chen sogs kyi chos skad thun mong ma yin pa las /
rang re dge ldan pa'i lugs la 'di dag lam gol ltar snang kho na las /
yang dag pa'i lam du 'jog pa rang lugs kyi mkhas grub tshad ldan su yang mi snang ba ma zad /
sems ngo 'phrod na las 'bras kyi spong len sogs mi dgos pa dang /
gang shar rnam rtog tsam yin tshul gyis bzang ngan sems tsam du smra ba dang /
sku gsum sku lnga sogs gzhi dus su rang chas su yod tshul smra 'di tsam ma zad deng dus grub mtha' gzhan phyogs pa'i mkhas blun phal mo che zhig gis /
ba 'di dag ni las 'bras khyad du bsad /
tshogs bsags sgrib sbyong sogs spyod phyogs kyi lam gyi rim pa mtha' dag 'dor zhing /
skur 'debs kyi mthar ltung ba dang /
ma dag pa'i phung khams la sku lnga sku bzhi sogs kyi sangs gzhi grub na don dam bden pa yin pas khyab 'dod pas /
kun rdzob mad par 'dzin pa'i chad lta mi bzad pa 'di ni /
gsung rab tshad ldan rnams nas dmyal ba mnar med kyi rgyur yang dang yang du gsungs pas luD ngan 'di dag la dug bzhin du 'dzem par bya dgos te /
rje phur lcog ngag dbang byams pa'i gsung las /
bod kyi blos byas theg pa mthon po rnams / /
mu stegs dang mtshungs rtag dngos yon tan kun / /
ye nas rdzogs pa sems can kun la yod / /
de nyid bla mas rang ngo sprad byas pas / /
ngo 'phrod tsam gyis sangs rgyas zhes brjod kyi / /
'di las mtshams rim pa med ces smra / /
deng sangs steng thams cad lugs 'dis khyab / /
rmongs dang le lo can la shin tu mkho / /
lta brtogs la las 'bras spang blang med / /
sngags pa rnams la spyod pa bkag pa med / /
ma dag 'khor ba med cing snod bcud kun / /
ye nas lha dang gzhal yas khang yin zer / /
ma dag las 'bras tshad mas ma grub pa'i / /
grub mtha' 'di ni chad lta'i mthar thug yin / /

e ma chos ltar bcos pas sangs rgyas bstan / /

rgyal ba'i shes rab @# / /
pha rol phyin la ma dad na / /
thos nas blo chung de yis 'di ni spong byed de / /
spangs nas skyabs med gyur pa de ni mnar med 'gro /
zhes chad lta sogs la zhen nas stong nyid kyi don phyin ci log tu bzung bas ni sher phyin zab mo'i don spangs te dmyal ba mnar med du 'gro bar gsungs shing /
'bri gung dpal 'dzin sogs kyis kyang 'di dag gi gnad go ba'i thabs su dgag sgrub kyi bslab bya yig 'jog mang du mjad pa don la gnas te /
thu'u bkwan chos kyi nyi ma'i gsung ke ta ka'i byi dor las sum ba mkhan chen dgag pa'i skabs su /
rgyal bo dar mas bstan pa bsnubs / /
de rjes chos log du ma 'phel / /
zhes pa 'bri gung dpal 'dzin gyi gsung du mdzad de /

gzhan yang /
kong po padma legs grub kyis /
rgyal bam lus pa thams cad kyi thugs ye shes khyab gdal gdod ma nas 'khrul ma myong ba'i gdod ma'i gnas lugs zhes sogs dris pa'i lan du /
brag sgro rab 'byams pas /
sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la 'khrul myong ba zhig ni nam gyi dus su'ang med /
de lta na'ang sems can byed ma myong bar sangs rgyas ba'i sangs rgyas 'phags pa ni shes bya la mi srid do / /
zhes dang /
shAkya thub pa sogs kyi thugs rgyud kyi ye shes chos sku yang thun mong ba'i rgyu dang /
thun mong min pa'i rgyu rnam par mi rtog pa dang /
mtshan dpe rnams kyang thun mong ba dang thun mong min pa'i rgyu bla ma bsu skyel sogs kyis sgrub dgos /
rang gi ngo bo 'di la ye gdod ma nas sangs rgyas su skyes pa sogs ni phyi rol pa'i 'dod par byed pas khas mi len lags /
zhes gsungs pa gzhan ngor mdzes chos ma mdzad pa'i bden par smra ba'i grub thob kyi gsung du 'dug pa shin tu yid ches pa'i gnas dang /
spyir mtha' yas pa'i gsung rab khungs ma rnams la gzu bo'i blos rtog dpyod 'jug ba ni rang gzhan la 'phral yun kun tu dge ba'i gnad che shos su snang ngo /
rgyas su zhen cing brloms pas rtag chad lam ngan gyi g.yangs chen por lam mchog tu zhen nas mi tshe hril po 'da' bar byed pa ni /
nyid kyi nyes pa sngar yod bshags sdom la mi phan par mi tshe stong zad kyi snon ma lta bur 'gyur nges pas /
de rigs la yid rton gang yang ma byas pa legs nges kho bos drang por lhag bsam bzang pos smras pa lags shing /
des na sdig pa sbyang thabs rang lugs mkhas grub tshad ldan gyi gsung du ma las byung ba ltar ltung bshags dang 'brel ba'i brkyang phyag /
rdor sems bsgom bzlas dang 'brel ba'i yig brgya /
mi 'khrugs pa'i gzungs sngags bzla ba sogs snying rus chen pos yun bsrings te shugs drag 'bad na sdig ltung tshan po che yang nges par 'dag par gdon mi za zhing /
sdig ltung 'dag pa'i rmi lam gyi mtshan ma yang 'byung bar 'gyur pas de lugs dang /
lhag par snyan brgyud kyi gsung rgyun du /
de snga sngags bla med kyi dbang chen thob cing sngags kyi sgor zhugs pa dag la so thar gyi pham pa sogs byung ba 'dag thabs thun mong ma yin pa bla med kyi dkyil 'khor gang yin pa de'i bdag 'jug len pa'am /
da'ang bskyar nas zhu ba sogs sngags sdom gso thabs la nan tan 'bad nas sngags sdom nyams ba sor chud na so thar gyi sdig ltung 'dag pa la shin tu stobs che bar gsungs pas de lugs nan tan dang /
dge sbyor yang byang chub lam gyi rim pa dang /
bde mchog yab bka' yum bka' gang rung zhig gi bzlas bsgom la brtson na gtan 'dun @# / /
snying po rab tu lon nges bcas de don thugs la bcang bar 'tshal / /

'jol zam gdong sprul sku mchog la stsal ba /
rje nyid nas gsung bris phebs pa'i dri ba dang por /
lam rim bshes gnyen bsten tshul la blo sbyangs skabs bshes gnyen bsten pa'i phan yon nas /
sbyor bas bsten tshul gyi bar yongs rdzogs la dpyad sgom thun gcig la tshang bar byed dgos sam /
thun dang por bsten pa'i phan yon tsam la dpyad sgom byed /
thun gnyis par ma bsten pa'i nyes dmigs la dpyad sgom byed /
thun gsum par rtsa ba dad pa sbyang ba sogs la dpyad sgom byed pa lta bu de 'dra byed chog gam /
yang dper na bsten pa'i phan yon lta bu la blo sbyangs skabs bde myur dang /
zhal lung /
bdud rtsi snying po sogs thams cad nas kha bskangs te thad kar sbyar nas bsgom e chog gsungs pa /
lam rim dmigs skor skyong skabs thun gcig la dmigs skor gyis bcad mang na shar sgom lta bu las gnad du mi 'gro bas /
des na dmigs skor sa bcad re re la'ang myong ba ma skyes kyi bar du zhag dang /
zla ba /
lo ji tsam gyi yun 'gor yang snyugs bsring ste skyong dgos pas /
bshes gnyen bsten pa'i phan yon dang bsten tshul log pa'i nyes dmigs gnyis rkyang pa la'ang lam rim che chung /
bde myur /
zhal lung sogs dang /
ma mtha' gtam rgyud tshun chad nas kha bskang /
rang gi rigs pas dpyad lugs rno khyad gang thon byas te myong ba ma thon gyi bar nyin zhag mang por gnad du bsnun te bskyang /
dmigs skor byings rtsa ba dang pa sbyang tshul nas 'jug sdom len pa'i bar shar sgom mdor bsdus tsam re /
phyin drug man la smon lam gyi yul tsam du byas nas skyong /
phan yon nyes dmigs bsam pa la myong ba thon na /
rtsa ba dad pa spyang ba'i sa bcad dang po bla ma sangs rgyas yin par rdo rje 'chang gis bzhed pa gcig pu la gnad du bkar nas skyong /
de la myong ba cung zad thon na /
gnyis pa 'phrin las kyi byed pa po yin pa la gnad du bkar nas skyong /
de sogs rim bzhin dmigs skor re re bzhin du gnad du bsnun nas skyong dgos /
'on kyang bshes gnyen bsten tshul gyi rtsa ba dad pa sbyang ba 'di myong ba thon pa shin tu dka' bas 'di la myong ba ma thon bar du 'di kho na la 'bad na phal pa rnams mi tshe hril por 'gor ba tsam gyis sa chod dka' bas bshes gnyen bsten tshul nas dmigs skor gcig dang /

mdo smad rgyal thang dgon la /
de ga dgon du rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'phags lugs dang /

des na rang re ri bo dga' ldan pa'i sngags kyi zab khyad thun mong ma yin pa ni gsang @# / /
bde 'jigs gsum ya ma bral bar nyams su len pa nyid yin par rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi gsung rjen pas 'jam mgon tsong kha pa chen por dngos su gdams pa'i gsung rgyun rje'i gsung 'bum du gsal ba ltar la| de yang mi slob pa'i zung 'jug gi go 'phang shin tu myur ba myur bar bsgrub pa'i dga' ldan snyan brgyud kyi bka' srol 'dri /
pha rgyud thams cad kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa la brten nas 'thob bya sangs rgyas kyi sku dag pa sgyu ma'i sku mtshan dpes sbras pa'i kha sbyor yan lag bdun ldan dang /
ma rgyud thams cad kyi rgyal po dpal 'khor lo bde mchog la brten nas 'thob bya sangs rgyas kyi thugs dag pa don gyi 'od gsal ye shes chos sku gnyis dus shin tu myur ba mi lo bcu gnyis tsam la 'grub par byed cing /
de dag gi 'gal rkyen sel phyir khyad chos lnga ldan rdo rje 'jigs byed dang bcas de gsum ya ma bral bar nyams su len dgos par gsungs /
rje btsun tsong kha pa chen po rang nyid kyis kyang nyin re bzhin du gsang bde 'jigs gsum ya ma bral bar rim gnyis dang bcas pa'i rnal 'byor nyams bzhes phyag len du btabs ba rje'i rnam thar chen mor gsal ba ltar lags na /

'jigs gsang sngon yod thog /
bde mchog zhig gsar 'dzugs thub na ci ma rung snyam snga lo rong sde rta mgrin tshe ring dngos 'phrad skabs dgon du bde mchog cho ga gsar 'dzugs kyi mchod thebs mthun rkyen phangs med gang nus phul te zhu brtsams dgos lugs nan mngags bgyis zin pas /

dus ji tsam snyigs pa tsam gyis byin rlabs je myur du 'gro ba dang /

'jam mgon snyan brgyud gsang ba'i mthar thug 'di lta bu la spyod du yod pa'i skabs 'dir phyi bshol dang le lor ma gyur pa'i thugs khur gang che zhig ci nas kyang brtson pa lhur bzhes mdzod / /

dwags po dga' rab rje drung blo bzang mkhyen rab la /

na mo gu ru /

sgo mtshams ma rnams dbang po'i sgo brgyad du bsgoms pas las rlung gi rgyu ba dang bor dbang po'i sgo brgyad nas nang du ldog pa dang /
de nas yul nyi shu rtsa bzhir dpa' bo dang dpa' mo rnams bsgoms pa'i stobs kyis rlung rnams yul nyer bzhi'i rtsa rnams su 'du ba dang /
de nas snying gar bde chen gyi 'khor lo'i lha rnams bsgoms pas rlung rnams snying ga'i rtsa 'dab brgyad du 'du ba dang| de nas dpyid thig rje btsun yab yum du bsgoms stobs kyis las rlung gi rgyu ba mtha' dag snying ga'i dpyid thig la thims pa sogs kyis rdzogs rim zab mo'i rtogs pa myur du 'dren pa'i smin byed khyad par can du 'gyur ba ste de ni zhal shes kyi khyad chos dang po dang /
gnyis pa ni /
rtsa gnas so sor bkod pa'i lus dkyil gyi lha rnams dpa' bo dang dpa' mo de dang de dngos yin snyam du bsgoms pas phyi'i yul nyer bzhi dang /
mkha' spyod sogs na bzhugs ba'i dpa' bo dang dpa' mo rnams rtsa gnas de dang der bzhugs nas byin gyis rlob pa ste de ni zhal shes kyi khyad chos gnyis pa dang /
gsum pa ni /
'di lta bu'i lus dkyil nyams su blangs bas mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis rang rigs kyi sgrub pa por gzigs te yid ltar myur ba'i shugs kyis byon nas lam gyi grogs mdzad de rtogs pa skye myur ba ni zhal shes kyi khyad chos gsum pa ste /
khyad chos gsum po de dag lus dkyil 'di gzhan las zab pa'i khyad chos su gsungs pa yin /
spyir bde mchog zab @# / /
pa'i khyad chos rnams kho bos kyang dpal 'khor lo sdom pa lus dkyil gyi chos skor dkar chag gi dbu'i tshigs bcad du bkod yod cing /
sle lung bzhad pa rdo rjes mdzad pa'i bde mchog bsnyen yig mkha' 'gro yi gsang mdzod du'ang zhib tu gsal ba lags / /

brag g.yab sgrol ma ri khrod pa dge sbyong grags pa la gnang ba /

ma mtha' chos ldan gyi lus su thugs smon nan tan mdzod /

sna rtser spro bsdu byas /

gtso bo sangs rgyas rdo rje chos su byed pa thun mong ma yin pa dang nang /
de la yum gyis 'khyud pa gsang ba'i lugs yin par thu'u bkwan rin po che'i gsung du yod /
sgrub thabs rgyas par dbang bzhi thun mong ma yin pa zhal las shes zhes pa thun mong ma yin pa'i dbang bzhi rgyas pa len tshul dga' ldan snyan brgyud ltar bya ba yin /

khyim gyi mi nor spyi la rab gnas dge legs char 'bebs yang yang dang /
rang yul gyi gtsug lag khang dang /
sku gsung thugs rten| dge 'dun gyi sde rnams la sri zhu bkur ste dang mchod sbrin gang nus bgyid cing /
las 'bras kyi blang dor la tshul bzhin du 'bad na bde skyid rim bzhin 'phel bar 'gyur ro / /
! char 'bebs par 'gro ba'i tshe /
chu mig so sor klu gnas min brtag pa ni /
chu mig khar mgo gtums la /
yi dam gyi sngags gsham du sngags 'di stong tsho gsum bzla'o / /
sngags ni /
nA ga ye swa ya swAhA /
zhes bzlas bas lus dang gdong cung 'phrig pa dang /
gyon pa dang lus la shig btsan thabs su @# / /
brgyag ba /
kha dang rna ba nas shig tshur 'ong ba sogs byung na klu gnas pa'i rtags dang /
cho 'phrul ma byung na klu mi gnas pa'i sa yin pas gzhan du spo bar bya'o / /
nus ldan gyi rtogs pas rtags byung ba'i tshe sngags rnams yun ring du bzlas na klu rnams skad ngan 'ong /
de byung ba dang ltab brtan bar byas la bcu re /
sngags 'di sbel nas 'don /
a ma tsa du a tri sa na sha mi g+hi rbad sod /
ces yid kyis mna' bsgag bas rang gis gang bcol nyan bar 'gyur ro /
sngags 'di phyis mi bzla'o / /
! sbrul sku rin po che nyid nas da lam ji ltar phebs pa'i don /
char 'bebs mdzad rgyu sgrol ma tsit+ta ma Ni 'di rang thugs rje 'phrin las ches myur /
kho bos char 'bebs snga phyi 'di'i sgo nas byas tshad la ma mtha' nyin lnga 'gyangs med char gyi rgyun chen po zhag mang babs pa sha stag byung ba myong grub la /
sku nyid nas kyang 'di'i sgo nas mdzad pa legs shing /
de yang gnas skabs ljags bsnyen rgyas pa ma grub kyang /
yi ge bcu pa 'bum phrag gcig kha skong zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bcas 'phral gnang gi thog nas /
snga lor zab khrid phul ba ltar de khul zin bris yod nges la yig cha dang phan tshun gung sgrig ste mdzad na 'thus /
skabs skabs su bdag mdun las 'od zer sbros te rgya mtsho las klu chen brgyad gdan drangs te nam mkha'i dbyings su khyab ste bzhugs pa'i sku las char sprin spro ba dang /
mdun bskyed las char sbrin stug po spros te nam mkha' khyab pa dang /
gzhan yang klu phran sdom dang /
sdig pa /
sbrul sogs kyis kyang sprin gyi bar rnams khyab par mos shing| yang klu rnams kyis lus sprugs pas char chen bo babs par mos kyang legs /
char 'bebs kyi cho ga ma bgyis pa'i skabs kyang rgyun gyi nyams len bla ma mchod pa'i tshogs zhing las thugs rje'i sprin phung spro ba dang /
klu 'gug pa sogs dmigs pa gong ltar byas pas kyang char 'bab pa la khyad che bar 'dug /
ngos nas kyang rgyun du skyabs 'jug stabs bde zhu mi rnams la 'di nyid rang gtso bor byed /
spyir char 'bebs sogs gtso bor spyi mthun gyi bsod nams dang /
dam tshig dang /
grub mtha' ris mi gcig pa dam sel yod rigs sogs kyis shin tu gnod che bar 'dug /
yang char bgegs zhi phyir char 'gong bsreg pa dang /
khro bcu'i srung 'khor bsgom pa dang /
chos skyong chen por bskang 'phrin sogs bsgrub na'ang gnad che bar snang| lar lo 'dir 'di ga rong por char rgyun mi chad du babs byung ba tsam las /
khyung po khul /
rgya ston khul /
sog khul tshang mar char shin tu dkon par byung 'dug pa spyi mthun gyi las rang yin 'dra yang /
bla ma lha dang /
chos skyong bcas kyi thugs rje bskul te thugs bskyed nan tan mdzad na mchog gsum slu ba med cing /
rgyu 'bras rten 'byung 'gog pa med pa'i 'bras bu gdon mi za bar 'byung nges lags pa dbyings rol /
'di'ang sho mdo grwa sgom sprul sku rin po che'i zhul na du gnang ba'o / /

zar 'bebs kyi gnad rim gal po che zhig la stsal ba /
phan bde'i sbrang char 'bebs dka' 'di dag gtso bo spyi mthun las dang /
lhag par char 'gong gis gnod rkyen yin nges la /
gnad dmigs rim gro /
byang sems nus ldan skyes bus char 'bebs kyi cho ga dang /

klu chog /
klu gtor /
klu'i rgyal po ma dros pa'i mdo chog gang rgyas /
bod ljongs klu chen grags che gang yod sar klu chog gnad smin /
yul gru so so nas gtor ma brgya rtsa dang 'brel ba'i lan chags gtor ma 'gro che /
dam tshig rdo rje'i bzlas pa bye ba /
bkra shis gso sbyong /
dkar phyogs lha klu yongs la bsangs khrus rgya che /
mi min 'byung po yongs la brngan dang gtor ma gang rgyas /
sde brgyad cha snyoms /
rang rang yul gru so sor rab tu gnas pa dge legs rgya mtsho'i char 'bebs bcas gnad bsnun 'bad tshe bzang ngo gsal ba de don chos klong du rol ba mkhyen|| ! / /
bar khams sho mdo dgon rdzong spyi la lo 'bras than bas gdungs ba gso ba'i skyabs lan du gnang ba /
'di lor yul phyogs phal cher du char rgyun shin tu dkon pa spyi mthun las bskos kyi myong bya ste /
skye 'gro phal cher gyis ser sna 'dod chen ngoms med du spyod pa las /
mchod sbyin bsod nams kyi skal ba dbul bo'i phye ltar phra ba dang /
lhag par lta grub chal chol sna tshogs 'dres ba'i dam sel dang /
dkar phyogs skyong ba'i lha klur nyams grib /
bcog grib sogs kyis gos shing nyams pa /
nag phyogs 'byung po rnams kyi mthu rtsal bdo ba sogs rgyu rkyen rten 'byung gi mthu sna tshogs shig 'dzoms pa las byung ba gdon mi za na /
gtso bor spyi mthun bsod nams gso phyir dkon mchog gi zhing la bsod nams kyi sa bon ci nus bskrun cing /
dge 'dun 'dus tshegs gang rgyas nas rab tu gnas pa dge legs rgya mtsho'i char 'bebs /
rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur dag sgrog /
yul gru so so'i rten gsum ri klung dang bcas par rten khrus yul khrus gang mang /
srung ma'i dbang po rnams kyi bskang 'phrin spyi dang /
khyad par rgyal chen rdo rje'i mtshan can gyi bskang tshogs 'gro che /
gnyug mar gnas pa'i gzhi'i bdag po yongs la bsangs dang gtor mas brngan pa /
sa bcud bum gter /
rang yul gyi mtsho klu chen gnas nges la gser sogs rin po che dang /
klu sman sogs kyis bkang ba'i gter bum 'dod gsol smon tshig dang bcas pa 'bul zhing /
klu gtor yang yang /
yul gru so sor brgya rtsa dang 'brel ba'i lan gter 'bum phrag bsngo ba /
skyes bu dam pa rnams nas klu chen brgyad kyi sbyin sreg dang /
klu chen gnas nges kyi mtsho khar char 'bebs kyi chog /
char 'gong bsreg mnan /
khro bcu'i srung zlog /
dge 'dun dag nas bkra shis gso sbyong dang /
khyim pa rnams nas kyang theg chen gso sbyong len zhing /
skyabs 'gro dang sgrol ma 'ur 'don bcas bsgrub na cung zad phan do dang /
gzhi rtsa rgyun du lo re bzhin sngon tshud nas 'di ltar gang nus bsgrub pa gal che ba bcas dgongs 'jags 'tshal / /

me byi lor chab mdo bla brang la gnang ba /
sbyir char chu dus babs /

nyi zla'i rang 'gros spyi 'gros /
sgra gcan gdong 'jug sogs rgyu skar dang 'dzoms gyes @# / /
kyi khyad par dang yul tsho so so'i ming skar 'phrad lugs sogs khyad par sna tshogs kyis /

zla ba 'di nang yul phyogs 'dir char babs dka' ba 'di dag kyang de lta'i khyad par sna tshogs kyis rkyen pa yin shag khar /
lhag par khul 'dir 'di lor zab rgyas chos kyi gru char sngar mi grags lta bu byung rkyen chos zab bdud sdang gis nag phyogs mi dang mi min 'byung po ci rigs kyis sgo kun nas glags tshol ci thub gang thub brtsams pa'ang gor ma chag pa bcas /

cha gsum /
maNi yi ge drug ma dang dmigs brtsem 'ur 'don bcas nan tan dang /
gzhi rtsa klu chog sbyor dngos rjes gtsang gnang bsnun 'bad mchog gsum bden mthu slu ba med pas char rgyun bzang bo rim bzhin 'beb par gdon mi za bas de lugs thugs la 'dog par mdzod / /
gzhan yang zhal gdams kyi rim pa sogs bka' rtsom ci rigs ba mang du yod pa las phal cher zhig bslab bya'i gras dang /
